There was NO jealousy, ego or greed. All were equal. Simple cheap pleasures, like just eating a lump of sugar made them happy. The old and aged were the happiest. Today these poor grandparents are the living and walking dead. &nbsp;Everybody is unhappy, including the rich in cars.<br />\n<br />\nThere was nothing called prostitution for money in Russia. <br />\n<br />\nAs young cadets, in the early seventies , I remember the fantastic days we had in Chevchenko Park of Odessa , ( Shivshankar for us ) a huge open air dance floor, with hundreds of pretty young Russian girls -- all wanting a dance, and some Wriggleys chewing gum, which we had in plenty in our bulging pockets. Indians were treated with love because India was the world's biggest democracy supporting \"so called\" evil Russia. We could come back to ship at 2 AM, the guards would allow us, all other nationalities went to the cooler.<br />\n<br />\nWhat follows here is some true information I received from a young gorgeous blue eyed Ukranian girl in Tel Aviv Riveria, whose house was near Chevchenko park , -- her mother had told stories of the open air dances.<br />\n<br />\nWell she was a trapped prostitute, with NO WAY OUT , who sat next to me in the open beer bar at the beach.<br />\n<br />\nLet me call her Natasha .&nbsp;She has this look of innocence. <br />\n<br />\nAt midnight this Tel Aviv beach is full of life and brightly lit like daylight, and the sea shimmers . My hotel was on the Riviera beach front, where I stayed 2 days. Natasha spoke English like a British lady, told me some horrifying stories, all true I guess , because she cried.<br />\n<br />\nBefore that let me digress , to my ship, form which I got down at Haifa. The agency has an Jewish Indian girl from Mumbai, and she loved to come on my ship and eat spicy Biriyani-- she was from Mumbai. She had told me that all Russian girls in Israel are home breakers, and that they all have affairs with married Jewish men . According to her the Russian girls chased men to be mistresses.<br />\n<br />\nThis was far from the stories Natasha told me--<br />\n<br />\nBefore that let me digress, --<br />\n<br />\nI went to the cabin of my Russian Third Mate, as part of a routine Captains Inspection. On his cabin bulkhead was a huge coloured poster or a gorgeous blue eyed beauty.<br />\n<br />\nI asked him &nbsp;\" Who is she? &nbsp;Is she a star in Russia, like &nbsp;Anna Kournikova\"?<br />\n<br />\nHe said \" No Captain, she is my wife!, We got married 2 months ago!\"<br />\n<br />\nAbout 2 weeks after that when I went on bridge to write my night orders , in the Third Mate's watch, I found that he had neglected certain routine and essential log entries in the GPS log.<br />\n<br />\nI got pissed off and demanded an explanation.<br />\n<br />\nHe said that he had a very long conversation with his wife, on Satcom phone , and that she had secured a amazingly well paying and good job outside Russia, and they were discussing the options.<br />\n<br />\nI said \" Tell me more! You are NOT off the hook yet !!\"<br />\n<br />\nThis job was offered to her by a Jewish Ex-Russian from Israel. And the whole strange thing was, that &nbsp;the broker did NOT want her to discuss it with her husband. The contract was for three months, and she would be home with pots of dollars, before her husband came back from ship. Her unmarried best friend was going too , and was eager that she also go along , so that two is company and comfort.<br />\n<br />\nI asked \" Have you seen her best friend? Is she beautiful like your wife ?\"<br />\n<br />\nHe said \" She is more beautiful. We all stayed since childhood in a huge housing complex having 500 families \"<br />\n<br />\nI asked him \" Did , you allow her?\"<br />\n<br />\nHe smiled \" Of course NOT! &nbsp;She will just disappear and will never come back home !! \"<br />\n<br />\nPatting his back I said &nbsp;\" Smart boy! Never mind that I just chewed you up\"-- and then went down to my cabin.<br />\n<br />\nTHE WHITE SLAVERY OF PRETTY YOUNG GIRLS IN ISRAEL IS NOT BEING ADDRESSED BY ANYBODY. <br />\n<br />\nFOR YOU CAN BE CALLED &nbsp;\" ANTI SEMITIC \" &nbsp;AND ROASTED FOR BEING RACIST. &nbsp; FOR JEWS ARE PROTECTED SPECIES LIKE PENGUINS , RIGHT?<br />\n<br />\nNatasha , I don't know if you are alive or dead--both ways, &nbsp;this post is dedicated to you--<br />\n<br />\nNatasha was lured to Israel using the bait of a well paid secretary job in a big company, as she spoke good English.<br />\n<br />\nSince her parents were living in abject poverty with ration coupons, and NO food at home, she said yes to the job. There was NO other way to improve the economic status . Her brother had gone into heavy drinking had a bad liver, and was irresponsible.<br />\n<br />\nShe qualified as a Israeli citizen, &nbsp;as her grand parents were Jews.<br />\n<br />\nOnce she arrived in Israel , by walking trough the Egyptian desert, her Passport with Visa was destroyed. Even before she crossed the border, she was raped. That was the first time she knew that all girls would be going into sex-trade-- the rapist told her so!<br />\n<br />\nUnlike other Russian prostitutes, she had a much better life, and lived in luxury , as she spoke excellent English, and was just 19 years old and beautiful. font-size: 12pt;\">A circa 350 AD hematite magic amulet, once in the collection of the Berlin Museum, depicted a man crucified on a cross with a moon and seven stars above his head and the words Orpheoc Bakkikoc.&nbsp;&nbsp;It was declared to be a forgery by a furious pope Pius XII.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The Orphic doctrine was purely vedic Indian and&nbsp;&nbsp;remained on a mythological plane, interpreting the universe in terms of personalized deities and procreation. Pythagoras refined and rationalized it and grabbed the glory later.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">A Indian Christian trader named Theophilos, from originally from Kerala and resident in Socotra island ( Aloe vera trade ) undertook several missionary journeys on behalf of the Roman emperor Constantius in the mid-4th century.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;He writes of a small Christian community in on the Malabar coast which traces its origins to Jesus' disciples Thomas and&nbsp;&nbsp;Bartholomew.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Bartholomew is one of the 12 disciples of Jesus and ismentioned in three Synoptic gospels: Matthew,[10:1\u20134] Mark,[3:13\u201319] and Luke,[6:12\u201316] and also appears as one of the witnesses of the Ascension[Acts 1:4,12,13]; however, each time he is named in the company of Philip.</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">He is not mentioned in Gospel of John.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">In the mid-6th century the Alexandrian merchant Kosmas Indikopleustes (India-navigator- TEE HEEEE ) is reputed to have visited the Malabar coast and Ceylon.&nbsp;&nbsp;Kosmas was the author of a stolen world-geography and a book on stolen Kerala astronomy.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">In his letter The Orphic Comparison of the Sun to God Ficino explains \u201cIt is certainly in the Sun that visible light is created from the light of consciousness, and there also sight is created from&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">understanding.&nbsp;&nbsp;For there understanding is no different from the light of consciousness, nor sight from visible light.\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Consciousness ?&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">TEEE HEEEE !<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">See, in a few paras I have trashed entire Greek history\u2014</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "4", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/37644750337536230/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "1144767609902667266", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-02-27T11:30:00+05:30", "updated": "2016-02-08T20:06:54+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNDU0OTQyMjE0NzgzCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/02/naive-sailor-locking-ig-tank-entry.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/1144767609902667266", "title": "THE NAIVE SAILOR , LOCKING IG TANK ENTRY VALVES -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-7uMtjDY19AE/TWnlJRwpX9I/AAAAAAAADvw/hWI_Ekhct58/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-7uMtjDY19AE/TWnlJRwpX9I/AAAAAAAADvw/hWI_Ekhct58/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nWhen i was a young Chief officer , I was on a ship with boiler flue INERT GAS , in 1980. In those days, none of the tankers had inert gas.<br />\n<br />\nYou may be surprised to know, that my first VLCC with IG was in 1976. My friends visited the ship from other tankers and were very surprised to see a funny looking thing on deck called deck seal and IG plant room.<br />\n<br />\nAs late as 1975, My ship a OBO used to load at Kharg Island ( Iran ) and Rastanura ( Saudi Arabia ) with a tape with wooden bob for ullaging. Topping up used to be with a T stick. Walkie talkies were NOT intrinsically safe. There were NO oxygen analysers and explosimeters.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-VScLNI__ZqE/TWnjwoNMBxI/AAAAAAAADvk/AlN0ldPMwa8/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-VScLNI__ZqE/TWnjwoNMBxI/AAAAAAAADvk/AlN0ldPMwa8/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nSo, the IG tank entry valves used to be Key Stone valves, which was basically a butterfly valve, operated by a lever, using a smooth 90 degree turn. There was NO spring loaded locking in click groove. This means that if the valve flap came under IG pressure, it would open by itself.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-chL432UFhv0/TWnj_Db167I/AAAAAAAADvo/_e_UhjK-Yz0/s1600/download+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-chL432UFhv0/TWnj_Db167I/AAAAAAAADvo/_e_UhjK-Yz0/s1600/download+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIn 1983, as a young Master, I wrote to certain important organisations, that the IG tank entry valves , must have a SPRING LOADED LOCKING ARRANGEMENT both in fully open and fully shut position, to avoid accidental opening by gas pressure.<br />\n<br />\nAnd I recommended that the swing type Key Stone valves must be replaced by a screw type butterfly valve, which can never be opened by gas pressure on the valve flap.<br />\n<br />\nTill then we had a locking arrangement retro installed &nbsp;, which could only be opened by a T shaped key, basically a spanner with socket, &nbsp;which we hung on the CCR bulkhead - tagged as the IG tank valve key.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-lD2cbzMAXQg/TWnkR9Eof0I/AAAAAAAADvs/Baw8Sj8Q2Ks/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-lD2cbzMAXQg/TWnkR9Eof0I/AAAAAAAADvs/Baw8Sj8Q2Ks/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe STUPID powers that be in IMO and OCIMF had taken this on the literal meaning.<br />\n<br />\n<b style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">This means, if a form had to be filled in </span><span style=\"font-size: x-large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">CAPITAL letters</span> </span><span style=\"font-size: large;\">or upper case letters, these cunts would take a flight to the </span><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: x-large;\">CAPITAL city</span><span style=\"font-size: large;\"> of their country, to fill it up.</span></b><br />\n<br />\nNow , let me jump fast forward to 2007.<br />\n<br />\n--after delivery of a brand new chemical tankers, built to Euro standards , with epoxy and zinc tanks, also designed for Crude oil and COW, we had to do 3 oil major vetting inspections. My European Chief officer was an Annex 1 man ,and it was his first Annex 2 ship. On his own he got 24 numbers padlocks fitted on all IG tank entry butterfly valve wheels with steel link chains. The 24 keys were kept in CCR.<br />\n<br />\nWhen i say 24 nos strange keys hanging on the CCR bulkhead , I asked him \" why have you LOCKED all IG valves with padlock and key? &nbsp;It is dangerous to do that \"<br />\n<br />\nHe said \" For the Oil Major Vetting , we require this or it will become a deficiency!\"<br />\n<br />\nI said \" But we already have a locking arrangement with a orifice and a spring loaded pin, in addition to these valves being rotary NOT swing , why do we need to lock it ? Remove it!\"<br />\n<br />\nSo my Chief officer removed all the padlocks-- all the time telling me ( he told me 4 times ) that it would be a deficiency, and that he has previous experience .<br />\n<br />\nSo , within a week I had an experienced and aged &nbsp;European nationality Vetting inspector for the No 1 Oil major of this planet , on board for the Vetting inspection.<br />\n<br />\nTo my surprise, he put down a deficiency ( there were only 3 total )-- IG TANK ENTRY INLET VALVES ARE NOT LOCKED , TO PREVENT UNAUTHORISED OPENING, --VIDE RULE SECTION NUMBER BLAH BLAH.<br />\n<br />\nMy red faced Chief officer smiled at me , in vindication-- as a sort of silent \" I told you so!\".<br />\n<br />\nI felt like a piece of s#it !!<br />\n<br />\nThere was NO way I could convince the STUPID vetting inspector, that locking with padlock and key is dangerous during cargo work at a Annex 1 or Annex 2 Terminal, in dim light at night or rain or snow .<br />\n<br />\nThere was NO way i could convince this A$$HOLE, that the IG inlet gas butterfly valves are worm spindle rotary valves, exactly like the liquid ones at the manifold.<br />\n<br />\nThere was NO way I could convince this IDIOT that the manifold liquid valves are subject to liquid hammer at 1000 times more pressure , than on a gas IG line , even then it is NOT required to lock these manifold valves.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-XiyIkGp7fY8/Tnchq89McuI/AAAAAAAAGSI/7Q6pdtIjqps/s1600/ndw.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-XiyIkGp7fY8/Tnchq89McuI/AAAAAAAAGSI/7Q6pdtIjqps/s1600/ndw.gif\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThere was NO way I could convince this MORON , that during cargo work on a tanker at an oil terminal there are NO unauthorised people like ship chandler or telephone card lady or barber , who will merrily go around opening valves , far away and below the catwalk like swinging monkeys.<br />\n<br />\nThere was NO way i could convince this NOT TOO BRIGHT inspector, that locking is NOT to prevent &nbsp;deliberate sabotage.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;
